## 1. [The New Kids (1985)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-new-kids-1985?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=the-new-kids-1985&utm_term=the-new-kids-1985)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-new-kids-1985?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=the-new-kids-1985&amp;utm_term=the-new-kids-1985"><img alt="the-new-kids-tt0089679-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/the-new-kids-tt0089679-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

In the crime-ridden town of Cedarville, a pair of newcomers bring their ingenuity, courage, and family values to help their struggling relatives run the beloved local amusement park. Infiltrating the close-knit community, the new kids unwittingly provoke the fury of a notorious local street gang, who have been terrorizing the town with their brutal crimes and malevolent intent. As tensions rise, our protagonists find themselves in the middle of a deadly battle against the ruthless gang, who are hell-bent on keeping their power and control over the town. They face unspeakable horrors and violent attacks that test their spirits, forcing them to reevaluate their beliefs in the face of evil. "The New Kids" is a gripping tale of innocence, corruption, and the fight for justice in a town plagued by the malevolent forces of the unknown. Filled with chilling suspense and gut-wrenching drama, this R-rated film is not for the faint of heart. Join our new kids as they stand up against the oppressive forces in their path and attempt to reclaim their innocence. 



<br>

- Genres: Crime, Drama, Horror
- Rated: R
- Runtime: 1h 50min
- Directed by: Sean S. Cunningham
- Starring: Shannon Presby, Lori Loughlin, James Spader

## 2. [Rock Odyssey (1987)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/rock-odyssey-1987?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=rock-odyssey-1987&utm_term=rock-odyssey-1987)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/rock-odyssey-1987?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=rock-odyssey-1987&amp;utm_term=rock-odyssey-1987"><img alt="rock-odyssey-tt1382663-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/rock-odyssey-tt1382663-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Rock Odyssey" (1987) is an animated musical adventure that combines the essence of love and rock music. The film's unique narrative style unfolds through the perspective of a sentient jukebox, as it guides Laura, a young woman, on a journey through four decades of 20th-century rock. As she searches for true love, the jukebox relives pivotal moments that defined the genre, providing a nostalgic soundtrack to Laura's quest. Packed with lively visuals, catchy tunes, and endearing characters, "Rock Odyssey" offers a delightful exploration of love and the power of music. Led by a talented ensemble of animators, directors, and lyricists, this Hanna-Barbera production is a must-watch for fans of both classic rock and animated films. 



<br>

- Genres: Animation, Music
- Runtime: 1h 12min
- Directed by: Joseph Barbera, William Hanna, Robert Taylor
- Starring: Scatman Crothers
- Box Office:
- IMDb Rating: 6.6

## 3. [Elvira: Mistress of the Dark (1988)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/elvira-mistress-of-the-dark-1988?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=elvira-mistress-of-the-dark-1988&utm_term=elvira-mistress-of-the-dark-1988)

Prepare for a wickedly entertaining journey in Elvira: Mistress of the Dark. This enchanting 1988 film follows the adventure of Elvira (Cassandra Peterson), a charismatic horror hostess who inherits a mysterious mansion in a small town. Elvira quickly finds herself entangled in a battle against her villainous uncle and the townspeople who seek to burn her at the stake. With her signature wisecrack humor and powerful magic, Elvira embarks on a darkly hilarious mission to uncover the town's deepest, most terrifying secrets. Join Elvira as she unites wit and charm in the face of evil, all while putting her own unique spin on the genre with her quirky charm. Don't miss the chance to experience Elvira: Mistress of the Dark, a thrilling and humorous cinematic experience unlike any other.

## 4. [Sundown: The Vampire in Retreat (1989)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/sundown-the-vampire-in-retreat-1989?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=sundown-the-vampire-in-retreat-1989&utm_term=sundown-the-vampire-in-retreat-1989)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/sundown-the-vampire-in-retreat-1989?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=sundown-the-vampire-in-retreat-1989&amp;utm_term=sundown-the-vampire-in-retreat-1989"><img alt="sundown-the-vampire-in-retreat-tt0098412-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/sundown-the-vampire-in-retreat-tt0098412-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Sundown: The Vampire in Retreat" is a peculiar and intriguing blend of comedy, horror, and western genres that showcases the lives of reclusive vampires in a small American town. The undead creatures don sun cream to protect themselves from daylight, and their tranquility is disrupted by the arrival of a descendant of Van Helsing. David Harrison, a scientist known for synthesizing transfusion blood, brings his family to the town of Purgatory, unaware of the underlying civil war amongst its residents. Sucked into the fray, Harrison's family must navigate a world of vampires led by Count Mardulak and Shane Dennis, who engage in a struggle over the traditional methods of obtaining blood. Amidst the chaos, Robert Van Helsing, a descendant of the famous vampire hunter, enters the scene adding to the hilarity and suspense of the situation. The film, directed by Anthony Hickox, promises a night of comedy during the bloodsucking, making it a must-watch for fans of urban fantasy with a cultish twist. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy, Horror, Western
- Rated: R
- Runtime: 1h 44min

[DuckTales the Movie: Treasure of the Lost Lamp (1990)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/ducktales-the-movie-treasure-of-the-lost-lamp-1990?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=ducktales-the-movie-treasure-of-the-lost-lamp-1990&utm_term=ducktales-the-movie-treasure-of-the-lost-lamp-1990)

Filled with awe-inspiring magic and the promise of a thrilling transformation, their journey leads them on a captivating hunt that's brimming with unexpected twists, hilarious misadventures, and of course, the beloved animated charm that fans of DuckTales and Disney have come to adore. ## 6. [My Cousin Vinny (1992)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/my-cousin-vinny-1992?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=my-cousin-vinny-1992&utm_term=my-cousin-vinny-1992)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/my-cousin-vinny-1992?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=my-cousin-vinny-1992&amp;utm_term=my-cousin-vinny-1992"><img alt="my-cousin-vinny-tt0104952-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/my-cousin-vinny-tt0104952-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"My Cousin Vinny" is a delightful and hilarious comedy-drama set in the rural South. The film follows two college-bound New Yorkers, Billy and Stan, who find themselves in deep trouble when they're falsely accused of murder during a stopover in Alabama. In a desperate bid for justice, they enlist the help of their uncouth and inexperienced cousin, Vinny, who just happens to be a loudmouth lawyer. As the trio navigate the unfamiliar judicial system, they must confront courtroom drama, unexpected twists, and their own misconceptions about the South. The movie is filled with uproarious comedy, heartfelt moments, and a surprising amount of legal savvy that leaves audiences cheering. Written by Dale Launer and directed by Jonathan Lynn, "My Cousin Vinny" stars Joe Pesci, Marisa Tomei, and Ralph Macchio. This groundbreaking film garnered widespread acclaim, winning one Oscar and receiving a total of five wins and six nominations. With a runtime of two hours, this movie is a perfect blend of humor and suspense that keeps viewers on the edge of their seats. If you're in the mood for some lighthearted comedy and unexpected twists in the courtroom, "My Cousin Vinny" is an unforgettable treat. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy, Crime
- Rated: R
- Runtime: 2h
- Directed by: Jonathan Lynn
- Starring: Joe Pesci, Marisa Tomei, Ralph Macchio

## 7. [We're Talkin' Serious Money (1992)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/were-talkin-serious-money-1992?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=were-talkin-serious-money-1992&utm_term=were-talkin-serious-money-1992)

<br>

"We're Talkin' Serious Money" is a 1992 comedy film directed by James Lemmo and written by Leo Rossi and James Lemmo. The film stars Dennis Farina, Leo Rossi, and Fran Drescher. Set in both New York and Los Angeles, the story follows the misadventures of two unlikely heroes who find themselves in hot water after losing $10,000 borrowed from a notorious mob boss. Their unexpected journey takes a surprising turn when they cross paths with a scandalous video involving senators in compromising positions. The duo is suddenly offered a cool million to acquire the incriminating footage, which sets off a thrilling series of twists and turns. As their bungling escapades ensue, the pair is constantly pursued by those who've discovered their involvement in the high-stakes scheme. But all is not as it seems, as a shocking surprise awaits on their journey to escape their precarious circumstances. Filled with laughs, suspense, and a touch of the absurd, "We're Talkin' Serious Money" is a hilarious comedy that pushes the boundaries of misadventures and mishaps. This PG-13 rated film is a must-watch for fans of humor and crime-infused comedies alike.

## 8. [Relentless 3 (1993)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/relentless-3-1993?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=relentless-3-1993&utm_term=relentless-3-1993)

Relentless 3, the thrilling sequel to the action-packed crime-drama, brings a new level of suspense to its viewers. Directed by James Lemmo and penned by Lemmo and Robison, this movie delivers top-notch entertainment with a star-studded cast, including Leo Rossi, William Forsythe, and Robert Costanzo. Set in Los Angeles, the relentless police detective, Sam Dietz, played by Leo Rossi, returns from self-imposed exile to assist the police in solving a series of brutal murders. To add a personal twist, the fiendish new serial killer targets Sam's latest love interest. As the investigation heats up, the stakes are raised, and the relentless hunter becomes the hunted. With a running time of 1 hour and 24 minutes, this action-packed crime drama will keep you on the edge of your seat. Featuring compelling plot twists and engaging performances, Relentless 3 promises an unforgettable cinematic experience that will leave you craving more. Prepare yourself for the ultimate thriller ride packed with intense action, dramatic twists, and a race against time in this suspenseful sequel. Relentless 3 may not be the most critically acclaimed film, with an IMDb rating of 5.1, but it sure knows how to keep you entertained. Its combination of thrilling action, edge-of-your-seat crime-drama, and gripping suspense make it a must-watch for fans of action, thriller, and suspense genres. So, gather your friends and family, and get ready for a night filled with heart-pounding excitement and sheer suspense with Relentless 3.

## 9. [I'm Mad (1994)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/im-mad-1994?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=im-mad-1994&utm_term=im-mad-1994)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/im-mad-1994?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=im-mad-1994&amp;utm_term=im-mad-1994"><img alt="im-mad-tt0110098-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/im-mad-tt0110098-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

Get ready to embark on a madcap adventure in the animated short, "I'm Mad" (1994), an unforgettable blend of musical numbers and comedic banter between the beloved Warner Brothers, Yakko and Wakko, and their spirited sister Dot. During a car ride with their psychiatrist Dr. Otto Scratchansniff, the trio showcases their signature wackiness and outrageous exploits as they star in their first theater short. This vibrant animated classic will have you enthralled in its surrealist humor and musical delight from start to finish. "I'm Mad" features the incomparable talents of Rob Paulsen, Jess Harnell, and Tress MacNeille, backed by rich storytelling from screenwriters Randy Rogel and Tom Ruegger. The film, directed by the visionary team of Rich Arons, David Marshall, and Audu Paden, is a testament to the enduring appeal of animated comedies and is brought to life through the exceptional animation of Warner Bros. "Horton Hears a Who! " (2008) is a heartwarming animated adventure comedy that takes you on a journey with Horton the Elephant, voiced by the hilarious Jim Carrey. Horton discovers a tiny microscopic community on a speck of dust called Whoville, inhabited by the Whos, who are no bigger than a speck of lint. However, his neighbors refuse to believe in their existence, leading Horton to embark on a quest to protect them. Directed by Jimmy Hayward and Steve Martino, Horton's story is brought to life through the writing talents of Cinco Paul, Ken Daurio, and Dr. Seuss. Featuring the likes of Steve Carell and Carol Burnett as voice talents, the movie is a delightful blend of humor, emotion, and adventure for all ages. With a budget of $85 million, "Horton Hears a Who! " managed to gross an impressive $298.5 million worldwide. The film received a 6.8 rating on IMDb and accumulated 148,647.0 votes. "Migration" is a heartwarming animated adventure released in 2023, starring Kumail Nanjiani, Tresi Gazal, and Elizabeth Banks. It's directed by the esteemed duo, Benjamin Renner and Guylo Homsy, and is a creation of Universal Pictures and Illumination Entertainment. The film promises a delightful fusion of computer animation and 3D rendering, making it visually captivating. The story revolves around a family of ducks, led by their overprotective father. Unable to enjoy life fully due to his father's excessive caution, the family plots to embark on an exciting vacation, a trip that is not only entertaining but also holds the promise of transforming their family dynamics. Despite the adversity, the film maintains an optimistic tone. Its genre composition, which includes Animation, Action, and Adventure, promises a compelling narrative filled with thrilling moments and lighthearted humor, making it perfect for viewers of all ages. "Migration" was met with acclaim, receiving a win and five nominations, affirming its standing as a quality family film. It's an entertaining and captivating visual spectacle, promising viewers an uplifting and unforgettable experience. So, if you are looking for an animated adventure that combines heartfelt family themes with exciting action scenes, "Migration" could be your next must-watch.
